## Description

#### What type of PR is this?
/kind bug

#### What this PR does / why we need it:

https://github.com/kubernetes-sigs/kueue/pull/8997#discussion_r2863877179

After pods are assigned to some node by topology assignment and before are ungated (and given nodeSelector for that specific node) it might happen that in between these two events a node can be tainted or become NotReady. In such scenario these pods would be stuck in Pending state as they are bound to a node by nodeSelector but will not be scheduled on a node because of a taint or NotReady condition.

Pods would be stuck like this and replacement pods would not be created because the existing pending pods are still waiting to be scheduled.


This PR introduces mechanism of waiting for all pods expected to be on a node. Only then when all pods are there we proceed with unhealthy node handling.

#### Which issue(s) this PR fixes:
Fixes #9616

#### Special notes for your reviewer:

#### Does this PR introduce a user-facing change?
<!--
If no, just write "NONE" in the release-note block below.
If yes, a release note is required:
Enter your extended release note in the block below. If the PR requires additional action from users switching to the new release, include the string "action required".
-->
```release-note
TAS: Fixed a bug where pods could become stuck in a `Pending` state during node replacement.
This may occur when a node gets tainted or `NotReady` after the topology assignment phase, but before
the pods are ungated.
```

## Reviews

### Review by [@mwielgus](https://github.com/mwielgus) (commented) — 2026-03-02T17:07:13Z

- **pkg/controller/tas/node_failure_controller.go:440** by [@mwielgus](https://github.com/mwielgus) — 2026-03-02T17:07:02Z
```diff
@@ -396,6 +423,44 @@ func (r *nodeFailureReconciler) reconcileWorkloadsOnNode(ctx context.Context, no
 	return result, nil
 }
 
+func classifyPodsForReplacement(pods []*corev1.Pod) (podsToTerminate []*corev1.Pod, hasPodsToRetain bool) {
+	for _, pod := range pods {
+		if !pod.DeletionTimestamp.IsZero() || utilpod.IsTerminated(pod) {
+			continue
+		}
+		if pod.Status.Phase == corev1.PodPending && !utilpod.HasGate(pod, kueue.TopologySchedulingGate) {
+			podsToTerminate = append(podsToTerminate, pod)
+		} else {
+			hasPodsToRetain = true
+		}
+	}
+	return
+}
+
+func (r *nodeFailureReconciler) terminatePods(ctx context.Context, pods []*corev1.Pod) error {
```

  The name of the function suggests that the pods are terminated. Yet, only the status of the pod is updated. Either:
  * delete the pod,
  * provide comment,
  * rename the funciton.

### Review by [@mwielgus](https://github.com/mwielgus) (commented) — 2026-03-02T17:09:57Z

- **pkg/controller/tas/node_failure_controller.go:528** by [@mwielgus](https://github.com/mwielgus) — 2026-03-02T17:09:57Z
```diff
@@ -453,6 +515,72 @@ func (r *nodeFailureReconciler) addUnhealthyNode(ctx context.Context, wl *kueue.
 	return nil
 }
 
+// isPodAssignedToNode checks if the pod is assigned to the node, either by being scheduled there
+// (spec.nodeName) or by having a TAS assignment that maps to this node (via nodeSelector).
+func isPodAssignedToNode(pod *corev1.Pod, nodeName string, levels []string) bool {
+	if pod.Spec.NodeName != "" {
+		return pod.Spec.NodeName == nodeName
+	}
+	if len(pod.Spec.NodeSelector) == 0 || len(levels) == 0 {
+		return false
+	}
+	key := levels[len(levels)-1]
+	val, ok := pod.Spec.NodeSelector[key]
```

  It is not always guaranteed that the lowest level of topology is node. What happens if it is not?

### Review by [@mimowo](https://github.com/mimowo) (commented) — 2026-03-04T17:41:30Z

- **test/e2e/tas/hotswap_test.go:540** by [@mimowo](https://github.com/mimowo) — 2026-03-04T17:41:30Z
```diff
@@ -498,6 +498,200 @@ var _ = ginkgo.Describe("Hotswap for Topology Aware Scheduling", ginkgo.Ordered,
 					expectPodsOnNodes(ctx, k8sClient, ns.Name, jobName, numPods, expectedNodes)
 				})
 			})
+
+			// In this test we use a job with SliceSize = 3 and SliceRequiredTopology = Block.
+			// Each pod requires 1 "extraResource" so the job will use three nodes from a Block.
+			// We simulate a node failure by making it NotReady while the pods are Pending (gated).
+			// The NodeFailureController should identify the pending pods assigned to the failed node and terminate them.
+			// The replacement mechanism should then find the available node in the same Block and replace the failed one.
+			// Note: This test verifies that NodeFailureController can act on pending pods that are assigned to the node (by the nodeSelector) but not scheduled yet.
+			ginkgo.It("Should replace a node when it becomes NotReady and pods are Pending", func() {
+				parallelism := 3
+				numPods := parallelism
+				jobName := "pending-notready-job"
+
+				// Use an artificial scheduling gate to keep pods pending
+				artificialGate := "kueue.x-k8s.io/dummy-gate"
+
+				sampleJob := testingjob.MakeJob(jobName, ns.Name).
+					Queue(kueue.LocalQueueName(localQueue.Name)).
+					Parallelism(int32(parallelism)).
+					Completions(int32(parallelism)).
+					Suspend(true).
+					PodLabel("job-name", jobName).
+					Obj()
+
+				sampleJob.Spec.Template.Spec.Containers = []corev1.Container{
+					{
+						Name:  "c",
+						Image: util.GetAgnHostImage(),
+						Args:  util.BehaviorWaitForDeletionFailOnExit,
+						Resources: corev1.ResourceRequirements{
+							Requests: corev1.ResourceList{
+								corev1.ResourceCPU: resource.MustParse("200m"),
+								extraResource:      resource.MustParse("1"),
+							},
+							Limits: corev1.ResourceList{
+								corev1.ResourceCPU: resource.MustParse("200m"),
+								extraResource:      resource.MustParse("1"),
+							},
+						},
+					},
+				}
```

  nit, I think we could we use the Wrapper (builders) for setting tat

### Review by [@mimowo](https://github.com/mimowo) (commented) — 2026-03-04T17:43:35Z

- **test/e2e/tas/hotswap_test.go:577** by [@mimowo](https://github.com/mimowo) — 2026-03-04T17:43:35Z
```diff
@@ -498,6 +498,200 @@ var _ = ginkgo.Describe("Hotswap for Topology Aware Scheduling", ginkgo.Ordered,
 					expectPodsOnNodes(ctx, k8sClient, ns.Name, jobName, numPods, expectedNodes)
 				})
 			})
+
+			// In this test we use a job with SliceSize = 3 and SliceRequiredTopology = Block.
+			// Each pod requires 1 "extraResource" so the job will use three nodes from a Block.
+			// We simulate a node failure by making it NotReady while the pods are Pending (gated).
+			// The NodeFailureController should identify the pending pods assigned to the failed node and terminate them.
+			// The replacement mechanism should then find the available node in the same Block and replace the failed one.
+			// Note: This test verifies that NodeFailureController can act on pending pods that are assigned to the node (by the nodeSelector) but not scheduled yet.
+			ginkgo.It("Should replace a node when it becomes NotReady and pods are Pending", func() {
+				parallelism := 3
+				numPods := parallelism
+				jobName := "pending-notready-job"
+
+				// Use an artificial scheduling gate to keep pods pending
+				artificialGate := "kueue.x-k8s.io/dummy-gate"
+
+				sampleJob := testingjob.MakeJob(jobName, ns.Name).
+					Queue(kueue.LocalQueueName(localQueue.Name)).
+					Parallelism(int32(parallelism)).
+					Completions(int32(parallelism)).
+					Suspend(true).
+					PodLabel("job-name", jobName).
+					Obj()
+
+				sampleJob.Spec.Template.Spec.Containers = []corev1.Container{
+					{
+						Name:  "c",
+						Image: util.GetAgnHostImage(),
+						Args:  util.BehaviorWaitForDeletionFailOnExit,
+						Resources: corev1.ResourceRequirements{
+							Requests: corev1.ResourceList{
+								corev1.ResourceCPU: resource.MustParse("200m"),
+								extraResource:      resource.MustParse("1"),
+							},
+							Limits: corev1.ResourceList{
+								corev1.ResourceCPU: resource.MustParse("200m"),
+								extraResource:      resource.MustParse("1"),
+							},
+						},
+					},
+				}
+				sampleJob.Spec.Template.Annotations = map[string]string{
+					kueue.PodSetPreferredTopologyAnnotation:     utiltesting.DefaultBlockTopologyLevel,
+					kueue.PodSetSliceRequiredTopologyAnnotation: utiltesting.DefaultBlockTopologyLevel,
+					kueue.PodSetSliceSizeAnnotation:             "3",
+				}
+				sampleJob.Spec.CompletionMode = ptr.To(batchv1.IndexedCompletion)
+				sampleJob.Spec.BackoffLimit = ptr.To[int32](1)
+
+				// Add the artificial scheduling gate to the pod template
+				sampleJob.Spec.Template.Spec.SchedulingGates = []corev1.PodSchedulingGate{
+					{Name: artificialGate},
+				}
+
+				util.MustCreate(ctx, k8sClient, sampleJob)
+
+				ginkgo.By("Job is unsuspended", func() {
+					gomega.Eventually(func(g gomega.Gomega) {
+						g.Expect(k8sClient.Get(ctx, client.ObjectKeyFromObject(sampleJob), sampleJob)).To(gomega.Succeed())
+						g.Expect(sampleJob.Spec.Suspend).Should(gomega.Equal(ptr.To(false)))
+					}, util.LongTimeout, util.Interval).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+				})
+
+				wlName := ""
+				ginkgo.By("Wait for topology assignment", func() {
+					gomega.Eventually(func(g gomega.Gomega) {
+						wls := &kueue.WorkloadList{}
+						g.Expect(k8sClient.List(ctx, wls, client.InNamespace(ns.Name))).To(gomega.Succeed())
+						g.Expect(wls.Items).To(gomega.HaveLen(1))
+						g.Expect(wls.Items[0].Status.Admission).NotTo(gomega.BeNil())
+						g.Expect(wls.Items[0].Status.Admission.PodSetAssignments).To(gomega.HaveLen(1))
+						g.Expect(wls.Items[0].Status.Admission.PodSetAssignments[0].TopologyAssignment).NotTo(gomega.BeNil())
+						wlName = wls.Items[0].Name
+					}, util.LongTimeout, util.Interval).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+				})
+
+				wlKey := client.ObjectKey{Name: wlName, Namespace: ns.Name}
+				initialNodes := []string{"kind-worker", "kind-worker2", "kind-worker3"}
```

  nit, could we easily read the nodes from the `TopologyAssignment`?

```diff
+			// In this test we use a job with SliceSize = 3 and SliceRequiredTopology = Block.
+			// Each pod requires 1 "extraResource" so the job will use three nodes from a Block.

+			ginkgo.It("Should replace a node when it becomes NotReady and pods are Pending", func() {

+					Completions(int32(parallelism)).
+					Suspend(true).
+					PodLabel("job-name", jobName).
+					Obj()
+

+						Image: util.GetAgnHostImage(),

+							},

+					kueue.PodSetSliceSizeAnnotation:             "3",
+				}
+				sampleJob.Spec.CompletionMode = ptr.To(batchv1.IndexedCompletion)
+				sampleJob.Spec.BackoffLimit = ptr.To[int32](1)
+
+				// Add the artificial scheduling gate to the pod template
+				sampleJob.Spec.Template.Spec.SchedulingGates = []corev1.PodSchedulingGate{
+					{Name: artificialGate},
+				}
+
+				util.MustCreate(ctx, k8sClient, sampleJob)
+
+				ginkgo.By("Job is unsuspended", func() {

+						g.Expect(k8sClient.Get(ctx, client.ObjectKeyFromObject(sampleJob), sampleJob)).To(gomega.Succeed())
+						g.Expect(sampleJob.Spec.Suspend).Should(gomega.Equal(ptr.To(false)))
+					}, util.LongTimeout, util.Interval).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+				})
+
+				wlName := ""
+				ginkgo.By("Wait for topology assignment", func() {
+					gomega.Eventually(func(g gomega.Gomega) {
+						wls := &kueue.WorkloadList{}
+						g.Expect(k8sClient.List(ctx, wls, client.InNamespace(ns.Name))).To(gomega.Succeed())
+						g.Expect(wls.Items).To(gomega.HaveLen(1))
+						g.Expect(wls.Items[0].Status.Admission).NotTo(gomega.BeNil())
+						g.Expect(wls.Items[0].Status.Admission.PodSetAssignments).To(gomega.HaveLen(1))

+									newGates = append(newGates, g)
+								}
```

```diff
+					}, util.LongTimeout, util.Interval).Should(gomega.Succeed())

+				for _, p := range pods.Items {

+				ginkgo.By(fmt.Sprintf("Simulate failure of node %s", nodeName), func() {

+						Type:   corev1.NodeReady,

+					for _, p := range pods.Items {
+						gomega.Eventually(func(g gomega.Gomega) {
+							updatedPod := &corev1.Pod{}
+							g.Expect(k8sClient.Get(ctx, client.ObjectKeyFromObject(&p), updatedPod)).To(gomega.Succeed())

+								}
```

```diff
+							g.Expect(k8sClient.Update(ctx, updatedPod)).To(gomega.Succeed())
+						}, util.Timeout, util.Interval).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+					}
+				})
+
+				var replacementPodName string
+				ginkgo.By("Wait for the victim pod to be Failed and the replacement pod to be created", func() {
+					gomega.Eventually(func(g gomega.Gomega) {
+						g.Expect(k8sClient.List(ctx, pods, client.InNamespace(ns.Name), client.MatchingLabels{
+							"job-name": jobName,
+						})).To(gomega.Succeed())
+
+						var victimPod *corev1.Pod
+						var replacementPod *corev1.Pod
+
+						for i := range pods.Items {
+							p := &pods.Items[i]
+							if p.Labels["batch.kubernetes.io/job-completion-index"] == "0" {
+								if _, ok := initialUIDs[string(p.UID)]; ok {
+									victimPod = p
+								} else {
+									replacementPod = p
+								}
+							}
+						}
+
+						g.Expect(victimPod).NotTo(gomega.BeNil(), "Victim pod should still exist")
+						g.Expect(victimPod.Status.Phase).To(gomega.Equal(corev1.PodFailed), "Victim pod should be Failed")
+						g.Expect(victimPod.Status.Conditions).To(gomega.ContainElement(gomega.BeComparableTo(corev1.PodCondition{
+							Type:   "TerminatedByKueue",
+							Status: corev1.ConditionTrue,
+							Reason: "UnschedulableOnAssignedNode",
+						}, cmpopts.IgnoreFields(corev1.PodCondition{}, "LastTransitionTime", "Message", "LastProbeTime"))), "Victim pod should have TerminatedByKueue condition with reason UnschedulableOnAssignedNode")
+
+						g.Expect(replacementPod).NotTo(gomega.BeNil(), "Replacement pod should appear")
+						replacementPodName = replacementPod.Name
+					}, util.LongTimeout, util.Interval).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+				})
+
+				ginkgo.By("Removing the artificial scheduling gate from the replacement pod", func() {
+					gomega.Eventually(func(g gomega.Gomega) {
+						updatedPod := &corev1.Pod{}
+						g.Expect(k8sClient.Get(ctx, client.ObjectKey{Name: replacementPodName, Namespace: ns.Name}, updatedPod)).To(gomega.Succeed())
+						foundArtificialGate := false
+						newGates := []corev1.PodSchedulingGate{}
+						for _, gate := range updatedPod.Spec.SchedulingGates {
+							if gate.Name == artificialGate {
+								foundArtificialGate = true
+							} else {
+								newGates = append(newGates, gate)
```

  Also this looks like one-liner with the helpers for ungating we have

```diff
+func classifyPodsForReplacement(pods []*corev1.Pod) (podsToTerminate []*corev1.Pod, hasPodsToRetain bool) {
+	for _, pod := range pods {
+		if !pod.DeletionTimestamp.IsZero() || utilpod.IsTerminated(pod) {
+			continue
+		}
+		if pod.Status.Phase == corev1.PodPending && !utilpod.HasGate(pod, kueue.TopologySchedulingGate) {
+			podsToTerminate = append(podsToTerminate, pod)
+		} else {
+			hasPodsToRetain = true
```

  This information is redundant, if you need it then declare the variable outside. You can just derive it by `hasPodsToRetain := len(input)  > len(podsToTerminate)`

```diff
-	return ListPodsForWorkloadSlice(ctx, r.client, wl.Namespace, workloadslicing.SliceName(wl))
+func (r *nodeFailureReconciler) checkPodsOnNode(ctx context.Context, nodeName string, wl *kueue.Workload, wlKey types.NamespacedName, untolerated []corev1.Taint, ready bool) (workloadHealthCheck, error) {
+	podsAssigned, hasGatedPods, err := r.getPodsAssignedToNode(ctx, wl, nodeName)
+	if err != nil {
+		return workloadHealthCheck{status: workloadHealthy}, fmt.Errorf("failed to get pods assigned to node %s: %w", nodeName, err)
+	}
+
+	if hasGatedPods && len(podsAssigned) == 0 {
```

  This feels flaky. What if the Pods are just not created yet. Then we will have `hasGatedPods=false`.
  
  So, I'm thinking we can step into `return workloadHealthCheck{status: workloadUnhealthy}, nil`, meaning replacing the Node, but without termination , and if the Pods get created just a little bit later before the replacement is done they may still land on the old node.
  
  One solution for such (rare) cases could be waitForPodsReady.recoveryTimeout, but I'm wondering if we could do better.
  
  So, I'm wondering we should wait for all Pods to be created here to collect them all for termination. We can determine the expected number of Pods based on the TopologyAssignment.
  
  Let me know if I'm missing something. Quite possible, because the logic here is rather tricky.

### Review by [@mimowo](https://github.com/mimowo) (commented) — 2026-03-04T18:28:46Z

- **pkg/controller/tas/node_controller.go:476** by [@mimowo](https://github.com/mimowo) — 2026-03-04T18:28:46Z
```diff
@@ -360,15 +378,21 @@ func (r *nodeFailureReconciler) reconcileWorkloadsOnNode(ctx context.Context, no
 
 	for wlKey := range allTASWorkloads {
 		var wl kueue.Workload
-		status, err := r.getWorkloadStatus(ctx, nodeName, node, wlKey, &wl)
+		result, err := r.getWorkloadStatus(ctx, nodeName, node, wlKey, &wl)
 		if err != nil {
 			return ctrl.Result{}, err
 		}
 
-		switch status {
+		if len(result.podsToTerminate) > 0 {
+			if err := r.markPodsFailed(ctx, result.podsToTerminate); err != nil {
+				return ctrl.Result{}, fmt.Errorf("marking pods as failed: %w", err)
+			}
+		}
```

  I have a doubt here - if there are multiple nodes for which the workload is unhealthy, eg. a disconnected rack, then we don't need to terminate the Pods at all - we could just rely on the eviction, right?
  
  I guess it is ok-ish, but if feasible I would like to limit the termination only to the pods when we have no choice.
  
  Let me know if you already analyzed that and concluded this is not easy. I guess it is ok-ish for Kueue to terminate them all, but it is also unnecessary work, because the eviction will trigger deletion of them anyway.

```diff
+func classifyPodsForReplacement(pods []*corev1.Pod) (podsToTerminate []*corev1.Pod, hasPodsToRetain bool) {
+	for _, pod := range pods {
+		if !pod.DeletionTimestamp.IsZero() || utilpod.IsTerminated(pod) {
+			continue
+		}
+		if pod.Status.Phase == corev1.PodPending && !utilpod.HasGate(pod, kueue.TopologySchedulingGate) {
+			podsToTerminate = append(podsToTerminate, pod)
+		} else {
+			hasPodsToRetain = true
```

  I think we need this because there is
  ```go
  if !pod.DeletionTimestamp.IsZero() || utilpod.IsTerminated(pod) {
  	continue
  }
  ```
  above and it filters some pods out.
  
  Let's say 3/4 pods succeeded and 1 is pending then with `hasPodsToRetain := len(input)  > len(podsToTerminate)` we would give invalid information

### Review by [@j-skiba](https://github.com/j-skiba) (commented) — 2026-03-10T10:54:42Z

- **test/e2e/tas/hotswap_test.go:540** by [@j-skiba](https://github.com/j-skiba) — 2026-03-10T10:54:42Z
```diff
@@ -498,6 +498,200 @@ var _ = ginkgo.Describe("Hotswap for Topology Aware Scheduling", ginkgo.Ordered,
 					expectPodsOnNodes(ctx, k8sClient, ns.Name, jobName, numPods, expectedNodes)
 				})
 			})
+
+			// In this test we use a job with SliceSize = 3 and SliceRequiredTopology = Block.
+			// Each pod requires 1 "extraResource" so the job will use three nodes from a Block.
+			// We simulate a node failure by making it NotReady while the pods are Pending (gated).
+			// The NodeFailureController should identify the pending pods assigned to the failed node and terminate them.
+			// The replacement mechanism should then find the available node in the same Block and replace the failed one.
+			// Note: This test verifies that NodeFailureController can act on pending pods that are assigned to the node (by the nodeSelector) but not scheduled yet.
+			ginkgo.It("Should replace a node when it becomes NotReady and pods are Pending", func() {
+				parallelism := 3
+				numPods := parallelism
+				jobName := "pending-notready-job"
+
+				// Use an artificial scheduling gate to keep pods pending
+				artificialGate := "kueue.x-k8s.io/dummy-gate"
+
+				sampleJob := testingjob.MakeJob(jobName, ns.Name).
+					Queue(kueue.LocalQueueName(localQueue.Name)).
+					Parallelism(int32(parallelism)).
+					Completions(int32(parallelism)).
+					Suspend(true).
+					PodLabel("job-name", jobName).
+					Obj()
+
+				sampleJob.Spec.Template.Spec.Containers = []corev1.Container{
+					{
+						Name:  "c",
+						Image: util.GetAgnHostImage(),
+						Args:  util.BehaviorWaitForDeletionFailOnExit,
+						Resources: corev1.ResourceRequirements{
+							Requests: corev1.ResourceList{
+								corev1.ResourceCPU: resource.MustParse("200m"),
+								extraResource:      resource.MustParse("1"),
+							},
+							Limits: corev1.ResourceList{
+								corev1.ResourceCPU: resource.MustParse("200m"),
+								extraResource:      resource.MustParse("1"),
+							},
+						},
+					},
+				}
```

```diff
+						g.Expect(k8sClient.Get(ctx, client.ObjectKeyFromObject(sampleJob), sampleJob)).To(gomega.Succeed())
+						g.Expect(sampleJob.Spec.Suspend).Should(gomega.Equal(ptr.To(false)))
+					}, util.LongTimeout, util.Interval).Should(gomega.Succeed())

+				wlName := ""
```

```diff
+			ginkgo.It("Should replace a node when it becomes NotReady and pods are Pending", func() {
+				parallelism := 3
+				numPods := parallelism
+				jobName := "pending-notready-job"
+
+				// Use an artificial scheduling gate to keep pods pending
+				artificialGate := "kueue.x-k8s.io/dummy-gate"
+
+				sampleJob := testingjob.MakeJob(jobName, ns.Name).
+					Queue(kueue.LocalQueueName(localQueue.Name)).
+					Parallelism(int32(parallelism)).
+					Completions(int32(parallelism)).
+					Suspend(true).
+					PodLabel("job-name", jobName).
+					Obj()
+
+				sampleJob.Spec.Template.Spec.Containers = []corev1.Container{
+					{
+						Name:  "c",
+						Image: util.GetAgnHostImage(),
+						Args:  util.BehaviorWaitForDeletionFailOnExit,
+						Resources: corev1.ResourceRequirements{
+							Requests: corev1.ResourceList{
+								corev1.ResourceCPU: resource.MustParse("200m"),
+								extraResource:      resource.MustParse("1"),
+							},
+							Limits: corev1.ResourceList{
+								corev1.ResourceCPU: resource.MustParse("200m"),
+								extraResource:      resource.MustParse("1"),
+							},
+						},
+					},
+				}
+				sampleJob.Spec.Template.Annotations = map[string]string{
+					kueue.PodSetPreferredTopologyAnnotation:     utiltesting.DefaultBlockTopologyLevel,
+					kueue.PodSetSliceRequiredTopologyAnnotation: utiltesting.DefaultBlockTopologyLevel,
+					kueue.PodSetSliceSizeAnnotation:             "3",
+				}
+				sampleJob.Spec.CompletionMode = ptr.To(batchv1.IndexedCompletion)
+				sampleJob.Spec.BackoffLimit = ptr.To[int32](1)
+
+				// Add the artificial scheduling gate to the pod template
+				sampleJob.Spec.Template.Spec.SchedulingGates = []corev1.PodSchedulingGate{
+					{Name: artificialGate},
+				}
+
+				util.MustCreate(ctx, k8sClient, sampleJob)
+
+				ginkgo.By("Job is unsuspended", func() {
+					gomega.Eventually(func(g gomega.Gomega) {
+						g.Expect(k8sClient.Get(ctx, client.ObjectKeyFromObject(sampleJob), sampleJob)).To(gomega.Succeed())
+						g.Expect(sampleJob.Spec.Suspend).Should(gomega.Equal(ptr.To(false)))
+					}, util.LongTimeout, util.Interval).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+				})
+
+				wlName := ""
+				ginkgo.By("Wait for topology assignment", func() {
+					gomega.Eventually(func(g gomega.Gomega) {
+						wls := &kueue.WorkloadList{}
+						g.Expect(k8sClient.List(ctx, wls, client.InNamespace(ns.Name))).To(gomega.Succeed())
+						g.Expect(wls.Items).To(gomega.HaveLen(1))
+						g.Expect(wls.Items[0].Status.Admission).NotTo(gomega.BeNil())
+						g.Expect(wls.Items[0].Status.Admission.PodSetAssignments).To(gomega.HaveLen(1))
+						g.Expect(wls.Items[0].Status.Admission.PodSetAssignments[0].TopologyAssignment).NotTo(gomega.BeNil())
+						wlName = wls.Items[0].Name
+					}, util.LongTimeout, util.Interval).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+				})
+
+				wlKey := client.ObjectKey{Name: wlName, Namespace: ns.Name}
+				initialNodes := []string{"kind-worker", "kind-worker2", "kind-worker3"}
+				ginkgo.By("Verify initial topology assignment of the workload", func() {
+					expectWorkloadTopologyAssignment(ctx, k8sClient, wlKey, numPods, initialNodes)
+				})
+
+				pods := &corev1.PodList{}
+				ginkgo.By("Wait for pods to be created and admitted (but still gated)", func() {
+					gomega.Eventually(func(g gomega.Gomega) {
+						g.Expect(k8sClient.List(ctx, pods, client.InNamespace(ns.Name), client.MatchingLabels{
+							"job-name": jobName,
+						})).To(gomega.Succeed())
+						g.Expect(pods.Items).To(gomega.HaveLen(numPods))
+						for _, p := range pods.Items {
+							g.Expect(p.Spec.SchedulingGates).To(gomega.ContainElement(corev1.PodSchedulingGate{Name: artificialGate}))
+						}
+					}, util.LongTimeout, util.Interval).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+				})
+
+				initialUIDs := map[string]struct{}{}
+				for _, p := range pods.Items {
+					initialUIDs[string(p.UID)] = struct{}{}
+				}
+
+				node := &corev1.Node{}
+				nodeName := initialNodes[0]
+				ginkgo.By(fmt.Sprintf("Simulate failure of node %s", nodeName), func() {
+					gomega.Expect(k8sClient.Get(ctx, client.ObjectKey{Name: nodeName}, node)).To(gomega.Succeed())
+					nodeToRestore = node.DeepCopy()
+					util.SetNodeCondition(ctx, k8sClient, node, &corev1.NodeCondition{
+						Type:   corev1.NodeReady,
+						Status: corev1.ConditionUnknown,
+					})
+				})
+
+				ginkgo.By("Removing the artificial scheduling gate from pods", func() {
+					for _, p := range pods.Items {
+						gomega.Eventually(func(g gomega.Gomega) {
+							updatedPod := &corev1.Pod{}
+							g.Expect(k8sClient.Get(ctx, client.ObjectKeyFromObject(&p), updatedPod)).To(gomega.Succeed())
+							newGates := []corev1.PodSchedulingGate{}
+							for _, g := range updatedPod.Spec.SchedulingGates {
+								if g.Name != artificialGate {
+									newGates = append(newGates, g)
+								}
+							}
+							updatedPod.Spec.SchedulingGates = newGates
+							g.Expect(k8sClient.Update(ctx, updatedPod)).To(gomega.Succeed())
+						}, util.Timeout, util.Interval).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+					}
+				})
+
+				var replacementPodName string
+				ginkgo.By("Wait for the victim pod to be Failed and the replacement pod to be created", func() {
```
```diff
+					gomega.Eventually(func(g gomega.Gomega) {
+						g.Expect(k8sClient.List(ctx, pods, client.InNamespace(ns.Name), client.MatchingLabels{
+							"job-name": jobName,
+						})).To(gomega.Succeed())
+
+						var victimPod *corev1.Pod
+						var replacementPod *corev1.Pod
+
+						for i := range pods.Items {
+							p := &pods.Items[i]
+							if p.Labels["batch.kubernetes.io/job-completion-index"] == "0" {
+								if _, ok := initialUIDs[string(p.UID)]; ok {
+									victimPod = p
+								} else {
+									replacementPod = p
+								}
+							}
+						}
+
+						g.Expect(victimPod).NotTo(gomega.BeNil(), "Victim pod should still exist")
+						g.Expect(victimPod.Status.Phase).To(gomega.Equal(corev1.PodFailed), "Victim pod should be Failed")
+						g.Expect(victimPod.Status.Conditions).To(gomega.ContainElement(gomega.BeComparableTo(corev1.PodCondition{
+							Type:   "TerminatedByKueue",
+							Status: corev1.ConditionTrue,
+							Reason: "UnschedulableOnAssignedNode",
+						}, cmpopts.IgnoreFields(corev1.PodCondition{}, "LastTransitionTime", "Message", "LastProbeTime"))), "Victim pod should have TerminatedByKueue condition with reason UnschedulableOnAssignedNode")
+
+						g.Expect(replacementPod).NotTo(gomega.BeNil(), "Replacement pod should appear")
+						replacementPodName = replacementPod.Name
+					}, util.LongTimeout, util.Interval).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+				})
+
+				ginkgo.By("Removing the artificial scheduling gate from the replacement pod", func() {
+					gomega.Eventually(func(g gomega.Gomega) {
+						updatedPod := &corev1.Pod{}
+						g.Expect(k8sClient.Get(ctx, client.ObjectKey{Name: replacementPodName, Namespace: ns.Name}, updatedPod)).To(gomega.Succeed())
+						foundArtificialGate := false
+						newGates := []corev1.PodSchedulingGate{}
+						for _, gate := range updatedPod.Spec.SchedulingGates {
+							if gate.Name == artificialGate {
+								foundArtificialGate = true
+							} else {
+								newGates = append(newGates, gate)
+							}
+						}
```

  Changes summary:
  
  - now we wait for all expected pods to be present on a node, when we finally have all of the expected pods on the node then we proceed with handling of an unhealthy node followed by optional stuck pending pods termination
  - late stuck pending pods that were recreated after termination of stuck pending by the node failure controller are handled by event based handling

  Wait, I think the new code should only be terminating Pods which are unschedulable. Such Pods by definition don't have NodeName. Terminating Pods with NodeName set is risky as it may mean killing Pods which are doing useful work.
  
  Unless, I'm missing something.

### Review by [@mimowo](https://github.com/mimowo) (commented) — 2026-03-10T19:09:18Z


  I think this is not going to work, because we may not see the "wl" to be already patched, because of the delay in the event propagation. Even if our controller sent the "eviction request" it still takes time to receive it back from the API server. That is why we check `if !evictedNow && !workload.IsEvicted(&wl) {` inside handleUnhealthyNode.

```diff
+func classifyPodsForReplacement(pods []*corev1.Pod) (podsToTerminate []*corev1.Pod, hasPodsToRetain bool) {
```

```diff
+					Queue(kueue.LocalQueueName(localQueue.Name)).
+					Parallelism(int32(parallelism)).
+					Completions(int32(parallelism)).
+					Suspend(true).
+					PodLabel("job-name", jobName).
+					Image(util.GetAgnHostImage(), util.BehaviorWaitForDeletionFailOnExit).
+					RequestAndLimit(corev1.ResourceCPU, "200m").
+					RequestAndLimit(extraResource, "1").

+					PodAnnotation(kueue.PodSetSliceSizeAnnotation, "3").
+					CompletionMode(batchv1.IndexedCompletion).
+					BackoffLimit(1).
+					SchedulingGate(artificialGate).
+					Obj()
+

+
+				ginkgo.By("Job is unsuspended", func() {
+					gomega.Eventually(func(g gomega.Gomega) {
+						g.Expect(k8sClient.Get(ctx, client.ObjectKeyFromObject(sampleJob), sampleJob)).To(gomega.Succeed())
+						g.Expect(sampleJob.Spec.Suspend).Should(gomega.Equal(ptr.To(false)))
+					}, util.LongTimeout, util.Interval).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+				})
+
+				wlName := ""
+				var topologyAssignment *kueue.TopologyAssignment

+						g.Expect(wls.Items[0].Status.Admission).NotTo(gomega.BeNil())
+						g.Expect(wls.Items[0].Status.Admission.PodSetAssignments).To(gomega.HaveLen(1))
+						g.Expect(wls.Items[0].Status.Admission.PodSetAssignments[0].TopologyAssignment).NotTo(gomega.BeNil())
+						wlName = wls.Items[0].Name
+						topologyAssignment = wls.Items[0].Status.Admission.PodSetAssignments[0].TopologyAssignment
+					}, util.LongTimeout, util.Interval).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+				})
+
+				wlKey := client.ObjectKey{Name: wlName, Namespace: ns.Name}
+				var initialNodes []string
+				for domain := range tas.InternalSeqFrom(topologyAssignment) {
+					initialNodes = append(initialNodes, domain.Values...)
+				}

+						}
+					}, util.LongTimeout, util.Interval).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+				})
+
+				initialUIDs := map[string]struct{}{}

+				}
```

```diff
+			// In this test we use a job with SliceSize = 3 and SliceRequiredTopology = Block.
+			// Each pod requires 1 "extraResource" so the job will use three nodes from a Block.
+			// We simulate a node failure by making it NotReady while the pods are Pending (gated).
+			// The NodeFailureController should identify the pending pods assigned to the failed node and terminate them.
+			// The replacement mechanism should then find the available node in the same Block and replace the failed one.
+			// Note: This test verifies that NodeFailureController can act on pending pods that are assigned to the node (by the nodeSelector) but not scheduled yet.
+			ginkgo.It("Should replace a node when it becomes NotReady and pods are Pending", func() {
+				parallelism := 3
+				numPods := parallelism
+				jobName := "pending-notready-job"
+
+				// Use an artificial scheduling gate to keep pods pending
+				artificialGate := "kueue.x-k8s.io/dummy-gate"
+
+				sampleJob := testingjob.MakeJob(jobName, ns.Name).
+					Queue(kueue.LocalQueueName(localQueue.Name)).
+					Parallelism(int32(parallelism)).
+					Completions(int32(parallelism)).
+					Suspend(true).
+					PodLabel("job-name", jobName).
+					Image(util.GetAgnHostImage(), util.BehaviorWaitForDeletionFailOnExit).
+					RequestAndLimit(corev1.ResourceCPU, "200m").
+					RequestAndLimit(extraResource, "1").
+					PodAnnotation(kueue.PodSetPreferredTopologyAnnotation, utiltesting.DefaultBlockTopologyLevel).
+					PodAnnotation(kueue.PodSetSliceRequiredTopologyAnnotation, utiltesting.DefaultBlockTopologyLevel).
+					PodAnnotation(kueue.PodSetSliceSizeAnnotation, "3").
+					CompletionMode(batchv1.IndexedCompletion).
+					BackoffLimit(1).
+					SchedulingGate(artificialGate).
+					Obj()
+
+				util.MustCreate(ctx, k8sClient, sampleJob)
+
+				ginkgo.By("Job is unsuspended", func() {
+					gomega.Eventually(func(g gomega.Gomega) {
+						g.Expect(k8sClient.Get(ctx, client.ObjectKeyFromObject(sampleJob), sampleJob)).To(gomega.Succeed())
+						g.Expect(sampleJob.Spec.Suspend).Should(gomega.Equal(ptr.To(false)))
+					}, util.LongTimeout, util.Interval).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+				})
+
+				wlName := ""
+				var topologyAssignment *kueue.TopologyAssignment
+				ginkgo.By("Wait for topology assignment", func() {
+					gomega.Eventually(func(g gomega.Gomega) {
+						wls := &kueue.WorkloadList{}
+						g.Expect(k8sClient.List(ctx, wls, client.InNamespace(ns.Name))).To(gomega.Succeed())
+						g.Expect(wls.Items).To(gomega.HaveLen(1))
+						g.Expect(wls.Items[0].Status.Admission).NotTo(gomega.BeNil())
+						g.Expect(wls.Items[0].Status.Admission.PodSetAssignments).To(gomega.HaveLen(1))
+						g.Expect(wls.Items[0].Status.Admission.PodSetAssignments[0].TopologyAssignment).NotTo(gomega.BeNil())
+						wlName = wls.Items[0].Name
+						topologyAssignment = wls.Items[0].Status.Admission.PodSetAssignments[0].TopologyAssignment
+					}, util.LongTimeout, util.Interval).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+				})
+
+				wlKey := client.ObjectKey{Name: wlName, Namespace: ns.Name}
+				var initialNodes []string
+				for domain := range tas.InternalSeqFrom(topologyAssignment) {
+					initialNodes = append(initialNodes, domain.Values...)
+				}
+				ginkgo.By("Verify initial topology assignment of the workload", func() {
+					expectWorkloadTopologyAssignment(ctx, k8sClient, wlKey, numPods, initialNodes)
+				})
+
+				pods := &corev1.PodList{}
+				ginkgo.By("Wait for pods to be created and admitted (but still gated)", func() {
+					gomega.Eventually(func(g gomega.Gomega) {
+						g.Expect(k8sClient.List(ctx, pods, client.InNamespace(ns.Name), client.MatchingLabels{
+							"job-name": jobName,
+						})).To(gomega.Succeed())
+						g.Expect(pods.Items).To(gomega.HaveLen(numPods))
+						for _, p := range pods.Items {
+							g.Expect(p.Spec.SchedulingGates).To(gomega.ContainElement(corev1.PodSchedulingGate{Name: artificialGate}))
+						}
+					}, util.LongTimeout, util.Interval).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+				})
+
+				initialUIDs := sets.New[string]()
+				for _, p := range pods.Items {
+					initialUIDs.Insert(string(p.UID))
+				}
+
+				node := &corev1.Node{}
+				nodeName := initialNodes[0]
+				ginkgo.By(fmt.Sprintf("Simulate failure of node %s", nodeName), func() {
+					gomega.Expect(k8sClient.Get(ctx, client.ObjectKey{Name: nodeName}, node)).To(gomega.Succeed())
+					nodeToRestore = node.DeepCopy()
+
+					// Stop kubelet so it doesn't immediately overwrite the condition
+					err := exec.Command("docker", "exec", nodeName, "systemctl", "stop", "kubelet").Run()
+					gomega.Expect(err).NotTo(gomega.HaveOccurred())
+
+					util.SetNodeCondition(ctx, k8sClient, node, &corev1.NodeCondition{
+						Type:   corev1.NodeReady,
+						Status: corev1.ConditionUnknown,
+					})
+				})
+
+				ginkgo.By("Removing the artificial scheduling gate from pods", func() {
+					for _, p := range pods.Items {
+						gomega.Eventually(func(g gomega.Gomega) {
+							updatedPod := &corev1.Pod{}
+							g.Expect(k8sClient.Get(ctx, client.ObjectKeyFromObject(&p), updatedPod)).To(gomega.Succeed())
+							if utilpod.Ungate(updatedPod, artificialGate) {
+								g.Expect(k8sClient.Update(ctx, updatedPod)).To(gomega.Succeed())
+							}
+						}, util.Timeout, util.Interval).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+					}
+				})
+
+				ginkgo.By("Wait for the victim pod to be Failed", func() {
+					gomega.Eventually(func(g gomega.Gomega) {
+						g.Expect(k8sClient.List(ctx, pods, client.InNamespace(ns.Name), client.MatchingLabels{
+							"job-name": jobName,
+						})).To(gomega.Succeed())
+
+						var victimPod *corev1.Pod
+
+						for i := range pods.Items {
+							p := &pods.Items[i]
+							if p.Labels["batch.kubernetes.io/job-completion-index"] == "0" {
+								if initialUIDs.Has(string(p.UID)) {
+									victimPod = p
+								}
+							}
+						}
+
+						g.Expect(victimPod).NotTo(gomega.BeNil(), "Victim pod should still exist")
+						g.Expect(victimPod.Status.Phase).To(gomega.Equal(corev1.PodFailed), "Victim pod should be Failed")
+						g.Expect(victimPod.Status.Conditions).To(gomega.ContainElement(gomega.BeComparableTo(corev1.PodCondition{
+							Type:   "TerminatedByKueue",
+							Status: corev1.ConditionTrue,
+							Reason: "UnschedulableOnAssignedNode",
+						}, cmpopts.IgnoreFields(corev1.PodCondition{}, "LastTransitionTime", "Message", "LastProbeTime"))), "Victim pod should have TerminatedByKueue condition with reason UnschedulableOnAssignedNode")
+					}, util.LongTimeout, util.Interval).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+				})
+
+				var replacementPodName string
+				ginkgo.By("Wait for the replacement pod to be created", func() {
+					gomega.Eventually(func(g gomega.Gomega) {
+						g.Expect(k8sClient.List(ctx, pods, client.InNamespace(ns.Name), client.MatchingLabels{
+							"job-name": jobName,
+						})).To(gomega.Succeed())
+
+						var replacementPod *corev1.Pod
+
+						for i := range pods.Items {
+							p := &pods.Items[i]
+							if p.Labels["batch.kubernetes.io/job-completion-index"] == "0" {
+								if _, ok := initialUIDs[string(p.UID)]; !ok {
+									replacementPod = p
+								}
+							}
+						}
```

  This look virtually like the code above: https://github.com/kubernetes-sigs/kueue/pull/9615/changes#diff-07939b70cb6f47dc8ed23bf44f1209770fd51fb091afc047fb4d8352b09c94e9R591-R602
  
  Can we have a helper for it?

```diff
+
```
```diff
+func expectPodWithIndex(ctx context.Context, k8sClient client.Client, nsName, jobName, index string, initialUIDs sets.Set[string], wantInitialUID bool, validateFn func(g gomega.Gomega, p *corev1.Pod)) *corev1.Pod {
+	var foundPod *corev1.Pod
+	gomega.EventuallyWithOffset(1, func(g gomega.Gomega) {
+		pods := &corev1.PodList{}
+		g.Expect(k8sClient.List(ctx, pods, client.InNamespace(nsName), client.MatchingLabels{
+			"job-name": jobName,
+		})).To(gomega.Succeed())
+
+		foundPod = nil
+		for i := range pods.Items {
+			p := &pods.Items[i]
+			if p.Labels["batch.kubernetes.io/job-completion-index"] == index {
+				if initialUIDs.Has(string(p.UID)) == wantInitialUID {
+					foundPod = p
+					break
+				}
+			}
+		}
```

```diff
 		if apierrors.IsNotFound(err) {

 	ready := utiltas.IsNodeStatusConditionTrue(node.Status.Conditions, corev1.NodeReady)

+

+		untolerated, temporarilyTolerated = classifyNoExecuteTaints(ctx, node.Spec.Taints, workload.PodSetsOnNode(wl, nodeName))
 		switch {
 		case len(untolerated) > 0:
 			if !features.Enabled(features.TASReplaceNodeOnPodTermination) {

+				return workloadHealthCheck{status: workloadUnhealthy}, nil
 			}
 			shouldWait = true
 		case len(temporarilyTolerated) > 0:
 			shouldWait = true
 		default:
-			return workloadHealthy, nil
+			return workloadHealthCheck{status: workloadHealthy}, nil
 		}
-	} else if !ready && features.Enabled(features.TASReplaceNodeOnPodTermination) {
+	case !ready && features.Enabled(features.TASReplaceNodeOnPodTermination):
 		// NotReady node
 		shouldWait = true
 	}
```

### Review by [@mimowo](https://github.com/mimowo) (commented) — 2026-03-12T06:49:05Z

- **pkg/controller/tas/node_controller.go:645** by [@mimowo](https://github.com/mimowo) — 2026-03-12T06:49:06Z
```diff
@@ -500,6 +610,66 @@ func (r *nodeReconciler) addUnhealthyNode(ctx context.Context, wl *kueue.Workloa
 	return nil
 }
 
+// isPodAssignedToNode checks if the pod is assigned to the node, either by being scheduled there
+// (spec.nodeName) or by having a TAS assignment that maps to this node (via nodeSelector).
+func isPodAssignedToNode(pod *corev1.Pod, nodeName string, levels []string) bool {
+	if pod.Spec.NodeName != "" {
+		return pod.Spec.NodeName == nodeName
+	}
+	if !utiltas.IsLowestLevelHostname(levels) {
+		return false
+	}
+	return pod.Spec.NodeSelector[corev1.LabelHostname] == nodeName
+}
+
+func getTopologyAssignmentLevelsForPod(pod *corev1.Pod, wl *kueue.Workload, psaMap map[kueue.PodSetReference]*kueue.PodSetAssignment) []string {
+	psName := kueue.PodSetReference(pod.Labels[constants.PodSetLabel])
+	psa, found := psaMap[psName]
+
+	// Fallback to the first assignment if the label is missing (common for simple/plain Pods)
+	if !found && len(wl.Status.Admission.PodSetAssignments) == 1 {
+		psa = &wl.Status.Admission.PodSetAssignments[0]
+		found = true
+	}
+
+	if found && psa.TopologyAssignment != nil {
+		return psa.TopologyAssignment.Levels
+	}
+
+	return nil
+}
+
+// getPodsAssignedToNode returns a list of pods that are assigned to the node (via spec.nodeName)
+// or are assigned by topology assignment but are not scheduled to the node (e.g. because of a taint).
+// It also returns a boolean indicating if there are any pods assigned to the Workload's topology
+// that are still gated by TopologySchedulingGate (missing nodeSelector).
```

  I think this function is conceptually very tricky because it mixes Pods which are assigned by TopologyAssignement with those which are bound via NodeName. These are very different classes of Pods, because we never want to terminate those which are bound (IIUC). So, I'm trying now to understand why we need both classes tracked, but also thinking if we could split them (return in separete slices). 
  
  I'm not yet committed to that view, because I still don't understand the code overall. Some explanation would help, trying to understand in the meanwhile .

### Review by [@mimowo](https://github.com/mimowo) (commented) — 2026-03-12T08:54:20Z

```diff
 	return result, nil

+func classifyPodsForReplacement(pods []*corev1.Pod, expectedOnNode int32) (podsToTerminate []*corev1.Pod, hasPodsToRetain bool) {
+	for _, pod := range pods {
+		if !pod.DeletionTimestamp.IsZero() || utilpod.IsTerminated(pod) {
+			continue
+		}
+		switch {
+		case expectedOnNode > 0 && pod.Status.Phase == corev1.PodPending && !utilpod.HasGate(pod, kueue.TopologySchedulingGate):
+			podsToTerminate = append(podsToTerminate, pod)
+		case expectedOnNode == 0:
+			// Orphaned late pods without any expected nodes must be terminated
+			podsToTerminate = append(podsToTerminate, pod)
```

  I think the only check relevant here is `pod.Status.Phase == corev1.PodPending` (together with the ` !pod.DeletionTimestamp.IsZero() || utilpod.IsTerminated(pod) ` checked already above

  I have a doubt we need this check. My understading is that after we added the podHandler we will be able to terminate Pods as they get created without the need to wait for all of them to accumulate. TBD

### Review by [@j-skiba](https://github.com/j-skiba) (commented) — 2026-03-12T11:43:47Z

- **pkg/controller/tas/node_controller.go:544** by [@j-skiba](https://github.com/j-skiba) — 2026-03-12T11:43:47Z

```diff
@@ -443,6 +531,48 @@ func (r *nodeReconciler) reconcileWorkloadsOnNode(ctx context.Context, nodeName
 	return result, nil
 }
 
+func classifyPodsForReplacement(pods []*corev1.Pod, expectedOnNode int32) (podsToTerminate []*corev1.Pod, hasPodsToRetain bool) {
+	for _, pod := range pods {
+		if !pod.DeletionTimestamp.IsZero() || utilpod.IsTerminated(pod) {
+			continue
+		}
+		switch {
+		case expectedOnNode > 0 && pod.Status.Phase == corev1.PodPending && !utilpod.HasGate(pod, kueue.TopologySchedulingGate):
+			podsToTerminate = append(podsToTerminate, pod)
+		case expectedOnNode == 0:
+			// Orphaned late pods without any expected nodes must be terminated
+			podsToTerminate = append(podsToTerminate, pod)
```

  done

```diff
+					Completions(int32(parallelism)).
+					Suspend(true).
+					PodLabel("job-name", jobName).
+					Image(util.GetAgnHostImage(), util.BehaviorWaitForDeletionFailOnExit).
+					RequestAndLimit(corev1.ResourceCPU, "200m").
+					RequestAndLimit(extraResource, "1").
+					PodAnnotation(kueue.PodSetPreferredTopologyAnnotation, utiltesting.DefaultBlockTopologyLevel).
+					PodAnnotation(kueue.PodSetSliceRequiredTopologyAnnotation, utiltesting.DefaultBlockTopologyLevel).
+					PodAnnotation(kueue.PodSetSliceSizeAnnotation, "3").
+					CompletionMode(batchv1.IndexedCompletion).
+					BackoffLimit(1).
+					SchedulingGate(artificialGate).
+					Obj()
+
+				util.MustCreate(ctx, k8sClient, sampleJob)
+
+				ginkgo.By("Job is unsuspended", func() {
+					gomega.Eventually(func(g gomega.Gomega) {
+						g.Expect(k8sClient.Get(ctx, client.ObjectKeyFromObject(sampleJob), sampleJob)).To(gomega.Succeed())
+						g.Expect(sampleJob.Spec.Suspend).Should(gomega.Equal(ptr.To(false)))
+					}, util.LongTimeout, util.Interval).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+				})
+
+				wlName := ""
+				var topologyAssignment *kueue.TopologyAssignment
+				ginkgo.By("Wait for topology assignment", func() {
+					gomega.Eventually(func(g gomega.Gomega) {
+						wls := &kueue.WorkloadList{}
+						g.Expect(k8sClient.List(ctx, wls, client.InNamespace(ns.Name))).To(gomega.Succeed())
+						g.Expect(wls.Items).To(gomega.HaveLen(1))
+						g.Expect(wls.Items[0].Status.Admission).NotTo(gomega.BeNil())
+						g.Expect(wls.Items[0].Status.Admission.PodSetAssignments).To(gomega.HaveLen(1))
+						g.Expect(wls.Items[0].Status.Admission.PodSetAssignments[0].TopologyAssignment).NotTo(gomega.BeNil())
+						wlName = wls.Items[0].Name
+						topologyAssignment = wls.Items[0].Status.Admission.PodSetAssignments[0].TopologyAssignment
+					}, util.LongTimeout, util.Interval).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+				})
+
+				wlKey := client.ObjectKey{Name: wlName, Namespace: ns.Name}
+				var initialNodes []string
+				for domain := range tas.InternalSeqFrom(topologyAssignment) {
+					initialNodes = append(initialNodes, domain.Values...)
+				}
```

  nit you can use slices.Collect to collect the sequence

### Review by [@mimowo](https://github.com/mimowo) (commented) — 2026-03-12T12:39:39Z

```diff
@@ -498,6 +472,156 @@ var _ = ginkgo.Describe("Hotswap for Topology Aware Scheduling", ginkgo.Ordered,
 					expectPodsOnNodes(ctx, k8sClient, ns.Name, jobName, numPods, expectedNodes)
 				})
 			})
+
+			// In this test we use a job with SliceSize = 3 and SliceRequiredTopology = Block.
+			// Each pod requires 1 "extraResource" so the job will use three nodes from a Block.
+			// We simulate a node failure by making it NotReady while the pods are Pending (gated).
+			// The NodeFailureController should identify the pending pods assigned to the failed node and terminate them.
+			// The replacement mechanism should then find the available node in the same Block and replace the failed one.
+			// Note: This test verifies that NodeFailureController can act on pending pods that are assigned to the node (by the nodeSelector) but not scheduled yet.
+			ginkgo.It("Should replace a node when it becomes NotReady and pods are Pending", func() {
+				parallelism := 3
+				numPods := parallelism
+				jobName := "pending-notready-job"
+

+				artificialGate := "kueue.x-k8s.io/dummy-gate"
+
+				sampleJob := testingjob.MakeJob(jobName, ns.Name).
+					Queue(kueue.LocalQueueName(localQueue.Name)).
+					Parallelism(int32(parallelism)).
+					Completions(int32(parallelism)).
+					Suspend(true).
+					PodLabel("job-name", jobName).
+					Image(util.GetAgnHostImage(), util.BehaviorWaitForDeletionFailOnExit).
+					RequestAndLimit(corev1.ResourceCPU, "200m").
+					RequestAndLimit(extraResource, "1").
+					PodAnnotation(kueue.PodSetPreferredTopologyAnnotation, utiltesting.DefaultBlockTopologyLevel).
+					PodAnnotation(kueue.PodSetSliceRequiredTopologyAnnotation, utiltesting.DefaultBlockTopologyLevel).
+					PodAnnotation(kueue.PodSetSliceSizeAnnotation, "3").
+					CompletionMode(batchv1.IndexedCompletion).
+					BackoffLimit(1).
+					SchedulingGate(artificialGate).
+					Obj()
+
+				util.MustCreate(ctx, k8sClient, sampleJob)
+
+				ginkgo.By("Job is unsuspended", func() {
+					gomega.Eventually(func(g gomega.Gomega) {
+						g.Expect(k8sClient.Get(ctx, client.ObjectKeyFromObject(sampleJob), sampleJob)).To(gomega.Succeed())
+						g.Expect(sampleJob.Spec.Suspend).Should(gomega.Equal(ptr.To(false)))
+					}, util.LongTimeout, util.Interval).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+				})
+
+				wlName := ""
+				var topologyAssignment *kueue.TopologyAssignment
+				ginkgo.By("Wait for topology assignment", func() {
+					gomega.Eventually(func(g gomega.Gomega) {
+						wls := &kueue.WorkloadList{}

+						g.Expect(wls.Items[0].Status.Admission.PodSetAssignments[0].TopologyAssignment).NotTo(gomega.BeNil())
+						wlName = wls.Items[0].Name
+						topologyAssignment = wls.Items[0].Status.Admission.PodSetAssignments[0].TopologyAssignment
+					}, util.LongTimeout, util.Interval).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+				})
+
+				wlKey := client.ObjectKey{Name: wlName, Namespace: ns.Name}
+				var initialNodes []string
+				for domain := range tas.InternalSeqFrom(topologyAssignment) {
+					initialNodes = append(initialNodes, domain.Values...)

+					expectWorkloadTopologyAssignment(ctx, k8sClient, wlKey, numPods, initialNodes)
+				})

+				ginkgo.By("Wait for pods to be created and admitted (but still gated)", func() {
+					gomega.Eventually(func(g gomega.Gomega) {
+						g.Expect(k8sClient.List(ctx, pods, client.InNamespace(ns.Name), client.MatchingLabels{
+							"job-name": jobName,
+						})).To(gomega.Succeed())
+						g.Expect(pods.Items).To(gomega.HaveLen(numPods))
+						for _, p := range pods.Items {
+							g.Expect(p.Spec.SchedulingGates).To(gomega.ContainElement(corev1.PodSchedulingGate{Name: artificialGate}))
+						}
+					}, util.LongTimeout, util.Interval).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+				})
+
+				initialUIDs := sets.New[string]()
+				for _, p := range pods.Items {
+					initialUIDs.Insert(string(p.UID))
+				}
```

  probably no need to cast to string, we can use typed UUID, and just collect to set, iirc sets.New(slices...)

```diff
+					SchedulingGate(artificialGate).

+					gomega.Eventually(func(g gomega.Gomega) {

+						g.Expect(sampleJob.Spec.Suspend).Should(gomega.Equal(ptr.To(false)))
+					}, util.LongTimeout, util.Interval).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+				})

+				wlName := ""

+				ginkgo.By("Wait for topology assignment", func() {
+					gomega.Eventually(func(g gomega.Gomega) {
+						wls := &kueue.WorkloadList{}
+						g.Expect(k8sClient.List(ctx, wls, client.InNamespace(ns.Name))).To(gomega.Succeed())
+						g.Expect(wls.Items).To(gomega.HaveLen(1))
+						g.Expect(wls.Items[0].Status.Admission).NotTo(gomega.BeNil())
+						g.Expect(wls.Items[0].Status.Admission.PodSetAssignments).To(gomega.HaveLen(1))
+						g.Expect(wls.Items[0].Status.Admission.PodSetAssignments[0].TopologyAssignment).NotTo(gomega.BeNil())

+				})
+
+				wlKey := client.ObjectKey{Name: wlName, Namespace: ns.Name}
+				var initialNodes []string
+				for domain := range tas.InternalSeqFrom(topologyAssignment) {
+					initialNodes = append(initialNodes, domain.Values...)
+				}
+				ginkgo.By("Verify initial topology assignment of the workload", func() {
+					expectWorkloadTopologyAssignment(ctx, k8sClient, wlKey, numPods, initialNodes)
+				})
+
+				pods := &corev1.PodList{}
+				ginkgo.By("Wait for pods to be created and admitted (but still gated)", func() {
+					gomega.Eventually(func(g gomega.Gomega) {
+						g.Expect(k8sClient.List(ctx, pods, client.InNamespace(ns.Name), client.MatchingLabels{
+							"job-name": jobName,
+						})).To(gomega.Succeed())
+						g.Expect(pods.Items).To(gomega.HaveLen(numPods))
+						for _, p := range pods.Items {
+							g.Expect(p.Spec.SchedulingGates).To(gomega.ContainElement(corev1.PodSchedulingGate{Name: artificialGate}))
+						}
+					}, util.LongTimeout, util.Interval).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+				})
+
+				initialUIDs := sets.New[string]()
+				for _, p := range pods.Items {
+					initialUIDs.Insert(string(p.UID))
+				}
+
+				node := &corev1.Node{}
+				nodeName := initialNodes[0]
+				ginkgo.By(fmt.Sprintf("Simulate failure of node %s", nodeName), func() {
+					gomega.Expect(k8sClient.Get(ctx, client.ObjectKey{Name: nodeName}, node)).To(gomega.Succeed())
+					nodeToRestore = node.DeepCopy()
+
+					// Stop kubelet so it doesn't immediately overwrite the condition
+					err := exec.Command("docker", "exec", nodeName, "systemctl", "stop", "kubelet").Run()
+					gomega.Expect(err).NotTo(gomega.HaveOccurred())
+
+					util.SetNodeCondition(ctx, k8sClient, node, &corev1.NodeCondition{
+						Type:   corev1.NodeReady,
+						Status: corev1.ConditionUnknown,
+					})
+				})
+
+				ginkgo.By("Removing the artificial scheduling gate from pods", func() {
+					for _, p := range pods.Items {
+						gomega.Eventually(func(g gomega.Gomega) {
+							updatedPod := &corev1.Pod{}
+							g.Expect(k8sClient.Get(ctx, client.ObjectKeyFromObject(&p), updatedPod)).To(gomega.Succeed())
+							if utilpod.Ungate(updatedPod, artificialGate) {
+								g.Expect(k8sClient.Update(ctx, updatedPod)).To(gomega.Succeed())
+							}
+						}, util.Timeout, util.Interval).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+					}
+				})
+
+				var victimPodName string
+				ginkgo.By("Wait for the victim pod to be Failed", func() {
+					gomega.Eventually(func(g gomega.Gomega) {
+						victimPod := findByPodIndex(ctx, k8sClient, g, ns.Name, jobName, "0", initialUIDs, true)
+						g.Expect(victimPod).NotTo(gomega.BeNil(), "Victim pod should still exist")
+						victimPodName = victimPod.Name
+					}, util.LongTimeout, util.Interval).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+					util.ExpectPodTerminatedByKueueCondition(ctx, k8sClient, client.ObjectKey{Name: victimPodName, Namespace: ns.Name}, "UnschedulableOnAssignedNode")
+				})
+
+				var replacementPodName string
+				ginkgo.By("Wait for the replacement pod to be created", func() {
+					gomega.Eventually(func(g gomega.Gomega) {
+						replacementPod := findByPodIndex(ctx, k8sClient, g, ns.Name, jobName, "0", initialUIDs, false)
+						g.Expect(replacementPod).NotTo(gomega.BeNil(), "Replacement pod should appear")
+						replacementPodName = replacementPod.Name
+					}, util.LongTimeout, util.Interval).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+				})
+
+				ginkgo.By("Removing the artificial scheduling gate from the replacement pod", func() {
+					gomega.Eventually(func(g gomega.Gomega) {
+						updatedPod := &corev1.Pod{}
+						g.Expect(k8sClient.Get(ctx, client.ObjectKey{Name: replacementPodName, Namespace: ns.Name}, updatedPod)).To(gomega.Succeed())
+						if utilpod.Ungate(updatedPod, artificialGate) {
+							g.Expect(k8sClient.Update(ctx, updatedPod)).To(gomega.Succeed())
+							g.Expect(utilpod.HasGate(updatedPod, artificialGate)).To(gomega.BeFalse(), "Still found artificial gate, retrying...")
+						}
+					}, util.Timeout, util.Interval).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+				})
+
+				ginkgo.By("Check that the topology assignment is updated with the new node in the same block", func() {
+					expectedNodes := slices.DeleteFunc([]string{"kind-worker", "kind-worker2", "kind-worker3", "kind-worker4"}, func(n string) bool {
+						return n == node.Name
+					})
+					gomega.Expect(expectedNodes).To(gomega.HaveLen(3))
```

  use initialNodes as the basis. Remove node.Name from the set and add `kind-worker4` to avoid repeating all node names.

```diff
+						}
+					}, util.Timeout, util.Interval).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+				})
+
+				ginkgo.By("Check that the topology assignment is updated with the new node in the same block", func() {
+					expectedNodes := slices.DeleteFunc([]string{"kind-worker", "kind-worker2", "kind-worker3", "kind-worker4"}, func(n string) bool {
+						return n == node.Name
+					})
+					gomega.Expect(expectedNodes).To(gomega.HaveLen(3))
```

  use initialNodes as the basis. Remove node.Name from the set and add `kind-worker4` to avoid repeating all node names.

### Review by [@mimowo](https://github.com/mimowo) (commented) — 2026-03-12T12:58:07Z

- **pkg/controller/tas/node_controller.go:651** by [@mimowo](https://github.com/mimowo) — 2026-03-12T12:58:07Z

```diff
+// isPodAssignedToNode checks if the pod is assigned to the node, either by being scheduled there
+// (spec.nodeName) or by having a TAS assignment that maps to this node (via nodeSelector).
+func isPodAssignedToNode(pod *corev1.Pod, nodeName string, levels []string) bool {
+	if pod.Spec.NodeName != "" {
+		return pod.Spec.NodeName == nodeName
+	}
+	if !utiltas.IsLowestLevelHostname(levels) {
+		return false
+	}
+	return pod.Spec.NodeSelector[corev1.LabelHostname] == nodeName
+}
+
+func getTopologyAssignmentLevelsForPod(pod *corev1.Pod, wl *kueue.Workload, psaMap map[kueue.PodSetReference]*kueue.PodSetAssignment) []string {
+	psName := kueue.PodSetReference(pod.Labels[constants.PodSetLabel])
+	psa, found := psaMap[psName]
+
+	// Fallback to the first assignment if the label is missing (common for simple/plain Pods)
+	if !found && len(wl.Status.Admission.PodSetAssignments) == 1 {
+		psa = &wl.Status.Admission.PodSetAssignments[0]
+		found = true
+	}
+
+	if found && psa.TopologyAssignment != nil {
+		return psa.TopologyAssignment.Levels
+	}
+
+	return nil
+}
+
+// getPodsAssignedToNode returns a list of pods that are assigned to the node (via spec.nodeName)
+// or are assigned by topology assignment but are not scheduled to the node (e.g. because of a taint).
+func (r *nodeReconciler) getPodsAssignedToNode(ctx context.Context, wl *kueue.Workload, nodeName string) ([]*corev1.Pod, error) {
```

  I would prefer to avoid mixing running pods and pending pods as results of the same function, because they are handled differently. 
  
  To detemine the list of "RUnning" pods we can use the already indexed spec.nodeName field at the controller runtime. iiuc we don't need full list of such pods, just information if there is at least one running, so that shouldWait answers true.
  
  To determine the list of Pending pods assigned to the node by topology assignement we could use our index, ie. indexPodNodeSelectorHostname

```diff
+type nodeFailurePodHandler struct {

+func (h *nodeFailurePodHandler) Create(_ context.Context, e event.CreateEvent, q workqueue.TypedRateLimitingInterface[reconcile.Request]) {
+	h.queueReconcileForPod(e.Object, q)
+}
+
+func (h *nodeFailurePodHandler) Update(_ context.Context, e event.UpdateEvent, q workqueue.TypedRateLimitingInterface[reconcile.Request]) {
+	h.queueReconcileForPod(e.ObjectNew, q)
+}
+
+func (h *nodeFailurePodHandler) Delete(_ context.Context, e event.DeleteEvent, q workqueue.TypedRateLimitingInterface[reconcile.Request]) {
+	h.queueReconcileForPod(e.Object, q)
+}
+
+func (h *nodeFailurePodHandler) Generic(_ context.Context, _ event.GenericEvent, _ workqueue.TypedRateLimitingInterface[reconcile.Request]) {
+}
+
+func (h *nodeFailurePodHandler) queueReconcileForPod(object client.Object, q workqueue.TypedRateLimitingInterface[reconcile.Request]) {
+	pod, isPod := object.(*corev1.Pod)
+	if !isPod {
+		return
+	}
+	if !utiltas.IsTAS(pod) {
+		// skip non-TAS pods
+		return
+	}
+
+	if pod.Status.Phase != corev1.PodPending {
+		// Only trigger the logic for situations when a pod is "late" and "pending"
+		return
+	}
+
+	nodeName := pod.Spec.NodeName
+	if nodeName == "" && pod.Spec.NodeSelector != nil {
+		nodeName = pod.Spec.NodeSelector[corev1.LabelHostname]
+	}
+
+	if nodeName != "" {
+		req := reconcile.Request{
+			NamespacedName: types.NamespacedName{
+				Name: nodeName,
+			},
+		}
+		q.Add(req)
```

  nit, would probably add some batch period here to avoid too many node reconciles in case multiple pods are ungated and are targeting the same node


  Actually, we don't need this extra check. From the scheduling perspective it does not matter if the Pod is "Running" phase or not. ### Review by [@mimowo](https://github.com/mimowo) (commented) — 2026-03-12T19:30:39Z

- **pkg/controller/tas/node_controller.go:639** by [@mimowo](https://github.com/mimowo) — 2026-03-12T19:30:39Z
```diff
@@ -500,6 +599,54 @@ func (r *nodeReconciler) addUnhealthyNode(ctx context.Context, wl *kueue.Workloa
 	return nil
 }
 
+// getPodsToTerminate returns a list of pending pods that are assigned to the node
+// (either scheduled or just assigned via topology), and a boolean indicating
+// if there is at least one pod to retain (e.g. running pod).
+func (r *nodeReconciler) getPodsToTerminate(ctx context.Context, wl *kueue.Workload, nodeName string) ([]*corev1.Pod, bool, error) {
+	sliceName := workloadslicing.SliceName(wl)
+
+	scheduledPods, err := ListPodsForWorkloadSlice(ctx, r.client, wl.Namespace, sliceName, client.MatchingFields{
+		"spec.nodeName": nodeName,
+	})
+	if err != nil {
+		return nil, false, fmt.Errorf("list scheduled pods: %w", err)
+	}
+
+	topologyAssignedPods, err := ListPodsForWorkloadSlice(ctx, r.client, wl.Namespace, sliceName, client.MatchingFields{
+		indexer.PodNodeSelectorHostnameKey: nodeName,
+	})
+	if err != nil {
+		return nil, false, fmt.Errorf("list topology assigned pods: %w", err)
+	}
+	var hasRunningPods bool
+	for _, pod := range scheduledPods {
+		if !pod.DeletionTimestamp.IsZero() || utilpod.IsTerminated(pod) {
+			continue
+		}
+		if pod.Status.Phase == corev1.PodRunning {
+			hasRunningPods = true
+			break
+		}
+	}
+
+	var podsToTerminate []*corev1.Pod
+	for _, pod := range scheduledPods {
+		if !pod.DeletionTimestamp.IsZero() || utilpod.IsTerminated(pod) {
+			continue
+		}
+		if pod.Status.Phase == corev1.PodPending && !utilpod.HasGate(pod, kueue.TopologySchedulingGate) {
+			podsToTerminate = append(podsToTerminate, pod)
+		}
```

  Yeah, we cannot terminate those - see the comment above. These pods might be already doing useful work, just pulling the image

```diff
+func (r *nodeReconciler) checkPodsOnNode(ctx context.Context, nodeName string, wl *kueue.Workload, untolerated []corev1.Taint, expectedOnNode int32) (workloadHealthCheck, error) {
+	podsToTerminate, hasRunningPods, err := r.getPodsToTerminate(ctx, wl, nodeName)

+// shouldWait encapsulates the logic for deciding if we need to
+// wait for pods to be fully created and assigned before declaring a node failure.
+func shouldWait(hasRunningPods bool, untoleratedCount int) bool {
+	if untoleratedCount == 0 {
+		return hasRunningPods
+	}
+
+	if hasRunningPods && features.Enabled(features.TASReplaceNodeOnPodTermination) {
+		return true
+	}
+
+	return false
```

### Review by [@mimowo](https://github.com/mimowo) (commented) — 2026-03-13T08:33:05Z

- **pkg/util/tas/tas_assignment.go:328** by [@mimowo](https://github.com/mimowo) — 2026-03-13T08:33:05Z
```diff
@@ -312,3 +312,40 @@ func ComputeUsagePerDomain(ta *TopologyAssignment, singlePodRequests resources.R
 	}
 	return usage
 }
+
+func ExpectedPodsOnNode(psa []kueue.PodSetAssignment, nodeName string) int32 {
+	var expected int32
+	for i := range psa {
+		psa := psa[i]
+		if psa.TopologyAssignment == nil {
+			continue
+		}
+		if !IsLowestLevelHostname(psa.TopologyAssignment.Levels) {
+			continue
+		}
+		for domain := range InternalSeqFrom(psa.TopologyAssignment) {
+			if len(domain.Values) > 0 && domain.Values[len(domain.Values)-1] == nodeName {
+				expected += domain.Count
+			}
+		}
+	}
+	return expected
+}
+
+func HasTASAssignmentOnNode(psa []kueue.PodSetAssignment, nodeName string) bool {
+	for i := range psa {
+		psa := psa[i]
+		if psa.TopologyAssignment == nil {
+			continue
+		}
+		if !IsLowestLevelHostname(psa.TopologyAssignment.Levels) {
+			continue
+		}
+		for domain := range InternalSeqFrom(psa.TopologyAssignment) {
+			if len(domain.Values) > 0 && domain.Values[len(domain.Values)-1] == nodeName {
+				return true
+			}
+		}
+	}
+	return false
+}
```

```diff
+	podsAssigned, err := r.getPodsAssignedToNode(ctx, wl, nodeName)

+		return workloadHealthCheck{status: workloadHealthUnknown}, fmt.Errorf("failed to get pods assigned to node %s: %w", nodeName, err)

+

+		// This node is not part of the workload's topology assignment. If pods are assigned
+		// here (e.g., late pods with old node selectors), they are stray and must be terminated.
+		return workloadHealthCheck{status: workloadHealthy, podsToTerminate: podsToTerminate}, nil
+	}
+
```

### Review by [@j-skiba](https://github.com/j-skiba) (commented) — 2026-03-16T07:19:06Z

- **test/e2e/tas/hotswap_test.go:556** by [@j-skiba](https://github.com/j-skiba) — 2026-03-16T07:19:06Z
```diff
@@ -498,6 +472,156 @@ var _ = ginkgo.Describe("Hotswap for Topology Aware Scheduling", ginkgo.Ordered,
 					expectPodsOnNodes(ctx, k8sClient, ns.Name, jobName, numPods, expectedNodes)
 				})
 			})
+
+			// In this test we use a job with SliceSize = 3 and SliceRequiredTopology = Block.
+			// Each pod requires 1 "extraResource" so the job will use three nodes from a Block.
+			// We simulate a node failure by making it NotReady while the pods are Pending (gated).
+			// The NodeFailureController should identify the pending pods assigned to the failed node and terminate them.
+			// The replacement mechanism should then find the available node in the same Block and replace the failed one.
+			// Note: This test verifies that NodeFailureController can act on pending pods that are assigned to the node (by the nodeSelector) but not scheduled yet.
+			ginkgo.It("Should replace a node when it becomes NotReady and pods are Pending", func() {
+				parallelism := 3
+				numPods := parallelism
+				jobName := "pending-notready-job"
+
+				// Use an artificial scheduling gate to keep pods pending
+				artificialGate := "kueue.x-k8s.io/dummy-gate"
+
+				sampleJob := testingjob.MakeJob(jobName, ns.Name).
+					Queue(kueue.LocalQueueName(localQueue.Name)).
+					Parallelism(int32(parallelism)).
+					Completions(int32(parallelism)).
+					Suspend(true).
+					PodLabel("job-name", jobName).
+					Image(util.GetAgnHostImage(), util.BehaviorWaitForDeletionFailOnExit).
+					RequestAndLimit(corev1.ResourceCPU, "200m").
+					RequestAndLimit(extraResource, "1").
+					PodAnnotation(kueue.PodSetPreferredTopologyAnnotation, utiltesting.DefaultBlockTopologyLevel).
+					PodAnnotation(kueue.PodSetSliceRequiredTopologyAnnotation, utiltesting.DefaultBlockTopologyLevel).
+					PodAnnotation(kueue.PodSetSliceSizeAnnotation, "3").
+					CompletionMode(batchv1.IndexedCompletion).
+					BackoffLimit(1).
+					SchedulingGate(artificialGate).
+					Obj()
+
+				util.MustCreate(ctx, k8sClient, sampleJob)
+
+				ginkgo.By("Job is unsuspended", func() {
+					gomega.Eventually(func(g gomega.Gomega) {
+						g.Expect(k8sClient.Get(ctx, client.ObjectKeyFromObject(sampleJob), sampleJob)).To(gomega.Succeed())
+						g.Expect(sampleJob.Spec.Suspend).Should(gomega.Equal(ptr.To(false)))
+					}, util.LongTimeout, util.Interval).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+				})
+
+				wlName := ""
+				var topologyAssignment *kueue.TopologyAssignment
+				ginkgo.By("Wait for topology assignment", func() {
+					gomega.Eventually(func(g gomega.Gomega) {
+						wls := &kueue.WorkloadList{}
+						g.Expect(k8sClient.List(ctx, wls, client.InNamespace(ns.Name))).To(gomega.Succeed())
+						g.Expect(wls.Items).To(gomega.HaveLen(1))
+						g.Expect(wls.Items[0].Status.Admission).NotTo(gomega.BeNil())
+						g.Expect(wls.Items[0].Status.Admission.PodSetAssignments).To(gomega.HaveLen(1))
+						g.Expect(wls.Items[0].Status.Admission.PodSetAssignments[0].TopologyAssignment).NotTo(gomega.BeNil())
+						wlName = wls.Items[0].Name
+						topologyAssignment = wls.Items[0].Status.Admission.PodSetAssignments[0].TopologyAssignment
+					}, util.LongTimeout, util.Interval).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+				})
+
+				wlKey := client.ObjectKey{Name: wlName, Namespace: ns.Name}
+				var initialNodes []string
+				for domain := range tas.InternalSeqFrom(topologyAssignment) {
+					initialNodes = append(initialNodes, domain.Values...)
+				}
+				ginkgo.By("Verify initial topology assignment of the workload", func() {
+					expectWorkloadTopologyAssignment(ctx, k8sClient, wlKey, numPods, initialNodes)
+				})
+
+				pods := &corev1.PodList{}
+				ginkgo.By("Wait for pods to be created and admitted (but still gated)", func() {
+					gomega.Eventually(func(g gomega.Gomega) {
+						g.Expect(k8sClient.List(ctx, pods, client.InNamespace(ns.Name), client.MatchingLabels{
+							"job-name": jobName,
+						})).To(gomega.Succeed())
+						g.Expect(pods.Items).To(gomega.HaveLen(numPods))
+						for _, p := range pods.Items {
+							g.Expect(p.Spec.SchedulingGates).To(gomega.ContainElement(corev1.PodSchedulingGate{Name: artificialGate}))
+						}
+					}, util.LongTimeout, util.Interval).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+				})
+
+				initialUIDs := sets.New[string]()
+				for _, p := range pods.Items {
+					initialUIDs.Insert(string(p.UID))
+				}
```

```diff
+					}, util.LongTimeout, util.Interval).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+				})
+
+				wlName := ""
+				var topologyAssignment *kueue.TopologyAssignment
+				ginkgo.By("Wait for topology assignment", func() {
+					gomega.Eventually(func(g gomega.Gomega) {
+						wls := &kueue.WorkloadList{}
+						g.Expect(k8sClient.List(ctx, wls, client.InNamespace(ns.Name))).To(gomega.Succeed())
+						g.Expect(wls.Items).To(gomega.HaveLen(1))
+						g.Expect(wls.Items[0].Status.Admission).NotTo(gomega.BeNil())
+						g.Expect(wls.Items[0].Status.Admission.PodSetAssignments).To(gomega.HaveLen(1))
+						g.Expect(wls.Items[0].Status.Admission.PodSetAssignments[0].TopologyAssignment).NotTo(gomega.BeNil())
+						wlName = wls.Items[0].Name
+						topologyAssignment = wls.Items[0].Status.Admission.PodSetAssignments[0].TopologyAssignment
+					}, util.LongTimeout, util.Interval).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+				})
+
+				wlKey := client.ObjectKey{Name: wlName, Namespace: ns.Name}
+				var initialNodes []string
+				for domain := range tas.InternalSeqFrom(topologyAssignment) {
+					initialNodes = append(initialNodes, domain.Values...)
+				}
+				ginkgo.By("Verify initial topology assignment of the workload", func() {
+					expectWorkloadTopologyAssignment(ctx, k8sClient, wlKey, numPods, initialNodes)
+				})
+
+				pods := &corev1.PodList{}
+				ginkgo.By("Wait for pods to be created and admitted (but still gated)", func() {
+					gomega.Eventually(func(g gomega.Gomega) {
+						g.Expect(k8sClient.List(ctx, pods, client.InNamespace(ns.Name), client.MatchingLabels{
+							"job-name": jobName,
+						})).To(gomega.Succeed())
+						g.Expect(pods.Items).To(gomega.HaveLen(numPods))
+						for _, p := range pods.Items {
+							g.Expect(p.Spec.SchedulingGates).To(gomega.ContainElement(corev1.PodSchedulingGate{Name: artificialGate}))
+						}
+					}, util.LongTimeout, util.Interval).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+				})
+
+				initialUIDs := sets.New[string]()
+				for _, p := range pods.Items {
+					initialUIDs.Insert(string(p.UID))
+				}
+
+				node := &corev1.Node{}
+				nodeName := initialNodes[0]
+				ginkgo.By(fmt.Sprintf("Simulate failure of node %s", nodeName), func() {
+					gomega.Expect(k8sClient.Get(ctx, client.ObjectKey{Name: nodeName}, node)).To(gomega.Succeed())
+					nodeToRestore = node.DeepCopy()
+
+					// Stop kubelet so it doesn't immediately overwrite the condition
+					err := exec.Command("docker", "exec", nodeName, "systemctl", "stop", "kubelet").Run()
+					gomega.Expect(err).NotTo(gomega.HaveOccurred())
+
+					util.SetNodeCondition(ctx, k8sClient, node, &corev1.NodeCondition{
+						Type:   corev1.NodeReady,
+						Status: corev1.ConditionUnknown,
+					})
+				})
+
+				ginkgo.By("Removing the artificial scheduling gate from pods", func() {
+					for _, p := range pods.Items {
+						gomega.Eventually(func(g gomega.Gomega) {
+							updatedPod := &corev1.Pod{}
+							g.Expect(k8sClient.Get(ctx, client.ObjectKeyFromObject(&p), updatedPod)).To(gomega.Succeed())
+							if utilpod.Ungate(updatedPod, artificialGate) {
+								g.Expect(k8sClient.Update(ctx, updatedPod)).To(gomega.Succeed())
+							}
+						}, util.Timeout, util.Interval).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+					}
+				})
+
+				var victimPodName string
+				ginkgo.By("Wait for the victim pod to be Failed", func() {
+					gomega.Eventually(func(g gomega.Gomega) {
+						victimPod := findByPodIndex(ctx, k8sClient, g, ns.Name, jobName, "0", initialUIDs, true)
+						g.Expect(victimPod).NotTo(gomega.BeNil(), "Victim pod should still exist")
+						victimPodName = victimPod.Name
+					}, util.LongTimeout, util.Interval).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+					util.ExpectPodTerminatedByKueueCondition(ctx, k8sClient, client.ObjectKey{Name: victimPodName, Namespace: ns.Name}, "UnschedulableOnAssignedNode")
+				})
+
+				var replacementPodName string
+				ginkgo.By("Wait for the replacement pod to be created", func() {
+					gomega.Eventually(func(g gomega.Gomega) {
+						replacementPod := findByPodIndex(ctx, k8sClient, g, ns.Name, jobName, "0", initialUIDs, false)
+						g.Expect(replacementPod).NotTo(gomega.BeNil(), "Replacement pod should appear")
+						replacementPodName = replacementPod.Name
+					}, util.LongTimeout, util.Interval).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+				})
+
+				ginkgo.By("Removing the artificial scheduling gate from the replacement pod", func() {
+					gomega.Eventually(func(g gomega.Gomega) {
+						updatedPod := &corev1.Pod{}
+						g.Expect(k8sClient.Get(ctx, client.ObjectKey{Name: replacementPodName, Namespace: ns.Name}, updatedPod)).To(gomega.Succeed())
+						if utilpod.Ungate(updatedPod, artificialGate) {
+							g.Expect(k8sClient.Update(ctx, updatedPod)).To(gomega.Succeed())
+							g.Expect(utilpod.HasGate(updatedPod, artificialGate)).To(gomega.BeFalse(), "Still found artificial gate, retrying...")
+						}
+					}, util.Timeout, util.Interval).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+				})
+
+				ginkgo.By("Check that the topology assignment is updated with the new node in the same block", func() {
+					expectedNodes := slices.DeleteFunc([]string{"kind-worker", "kind-worker2", "kind-worker3", "kind-worker4"}, func(n string) bool {
+						return n == node.Name
+					})
+					gomega.Expect(expectedNodes).To(gomega.HaveLen(3))
```

```diff
+// isPodAssignedToNode checks if the pod is assigned to the node, either by being scheduled there
+// (spec.nodeName) or by having a TAS assignment that maps to this node (via nodeSelector).
+func isPodAssignedToNode(pod *corev1.Pod, nodeName string, levels []string) bool {
+	if pod.Spec.NodeName != "" {
+		return pod.Spec.NodeName == nodeName
+	}
+	if !utiltas.IsLowestLevelHostname(levels) {
+		return false
+	}
+	return pod.Spec.NodeSelector[corev1.LabelHostname] == nodeName
+}
+
+func getTopologyAssignmentLevelsForPod(pod *corev1.Pod, wl *kueue.Workload, psaMap map[kueue.PodSetReference]*kueue.PodSetAssignment) []string {
+	psName := kueue.PodSetReference(pod.Labels[constants.PodSetLabel])
+	psa, found := psaMap[psName]
+
+	// Fallback to the first assignment if the label is missing (common for simple/plain Pods)
+	if !found && len(wl.Status.Admission.PodSetAssignments) == 1 {
+		psa = &wl.Status.Admission.PodSetAssignments[0]
+		found = true
+	}
+
+	if found && psa.TopologyAssignment != nil {
+		return psa.TopologyAssignment.Levels
+	}
+
+	return nil
+}
+
+// getPodsAssignedToNode returns a list of pods that are assigned to the node (via spec.nodeName)
+// or are assigned by topology assignment but are not scheduled to the node (e.g. because of a taint).
+func (r *nodeReconciler) getPodsAssignedToNode(ctx context.Context, wl *kueue.Workload, nodeName string) ([]*corev1.Pod, error) {
```

  I refactored this into 
  ```go
  // getPodsToTerminate returns a list of pending pods that are assigned to the node by topology (but not yet scheduled),
  // and a boolean indicating if there is at least one pod to retain (e.g. any scheduled pod).
  func (r *nodeReconciler) getPodsToTerminate(ctx context.Context, wl *kueue.Workload, nodeName string) ([]*corev1.Pod, bool, error)
  ```

  and now they are using the both indexers to list the pods

```diff
+type nodeFailurePodHandler struct {
+	client client.Client

+
+func (h *nodeFailurePodHandler) Create(_ context.Context, e event.CreateEvent, q workqueue.TypedRateLimitingInterface[reconcile.Request]) {
+	h.queueReconcileForPod(e.Object, q)
+}
+
+func (h *nodeFailurePodHandler) Update(_ context.Context, e event.UpdateEvent, q workqueue.TypedRateLimitingInterface[reconcile.Request]) {
+	h.queueReconcileForPod(e.ObjectNew, q)
+}
+
+func (h *nodeFailurePodHandler) Delete(_ context.Context, e event.DeleteEvent, q workqueue.TypedRateLimitingInterface[reconcile.Request]) {
+	h.queueReconcileForPod(e.Object, q)
+}
+
+func (h *nodeFailurePodHandler) Generic(_ context.Context, _ event.GenericEvent, _ workqueue.TypedRateLimitingInterface[reconcile.Request]) {
+}
+
+func (h *nodeFailurePodHandler) queueReconcileForPod(object client.Object, q workqueue.TypedRateLimitingInterface[reconcile.Request]) {
+	pod, isPod := object.(*corev1.Pod)
+	if !isPod {
+		return
+	}
+	if !utiltas.IsTAS(pod) {
+		// skip non-TAS pods
+		return
+	}
+
+	if pod.Status.Phase != corev1.PodPending {
+		// Only trigger the logic for situations when a pod is "late" and "pending"
+		return
+	}
+
+	nodeName := pod.Spec.NodeName
+	if nodeName == "" && pod.Spec.NodeSelector != nil {
+		nodeName = pod.Spec.NodeSelector[corev1.LabelHostname]
+	}
+
+	if nodeName != "" {
+		req := reconcile.Request{
+			NamespacedName: types.NamespacedName{
+				Name: nodeName,
+			},
+		}
+		q.Add(req)
```

  added 100ms batch period

```diff
+		return nil, false, fmt.Errorf("list topology assigned pods: %w", err)
+	}
+	var hasRunningPods bool
+	for _, pod := range scheduledPods {
+		if !pod.DeletionTimestamp.IsZero() || utilpod.IsTerminated(pod) {
+			continue
+		}
+		if pod.Status.Phase == corev1.PodRunning {
```

```diff
+func ExpectedPodsOnNode(psa []kueue.PodSetAssignment, nodeName string) int32 {
+	var expected int32
+	for i := range psa {
+		psa := psa[i]
+		if psa.TopologyAssignment == nil {
+			continue
+		}
+		if !IsLowestLevelHostname(psa.TopologyAssignment.Levels) {
+			continue
+		}
+		for domain := range InternalSeqFrom(psa.TopologyAssignment) {
+			if len(domain.Values) > 0 && domain.Values[len(domain.Values)-1] == nodeName {
+				expected += domain.Count
+			}
+		}
+	}
+	return expected
```

- **pkg/controller/tas/indexer/indexer.go:63** by [@olekzabl](https://github.com/olekzabl) — 2026-03-13T12:33:28Z
```diff

 	return []string{value}
 }
 
+func indexPodNodeSelectorHostname(o client.Object) []string {
+	pod, ok := o.(*corev1.Pod)
+	if !ok || !utiltas.IsTAS(pod) {
+		return nil
+	}
+	if pod.Spec.NodeSelector != nil && pod.Spec.NodeName == "" {
```

  I'm concerned about the `&& pod.Spec.NodeName == ""` part.
  
  I understand it makes the indexing a bit lighter (assuming we currently need the index only for pods satisfying this condition).
  OTOH, this creates a readability issue (a potential surprise): in the future, someone else might want to search for Pods by `spec.nodeSelector`, and expect _all_ matching results there.
  
  WDYT? Are there precedents in the code for such "non-trivial indexes"?
